[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Java-based fuzzing session has uncovered an out-of-memory condition when [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing certain PDF files. The crash is identified as [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`, surfaced through a [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“FuzzerSecurityIssueLow” exception. The failure occurs deep in the PDFBox [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfont‐parsing pipeline when handling a PFB [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPrinter Font Binary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m resource, causing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muncontrolled memory growth and eventual heap exhaustion.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing of a PDF text extraction harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe application runs out of Java heap space while parsing Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font data in PFB [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat. The fuzzer’s input triggers an exceptionally large or malformed PFB stream [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat overflows available memory, resulting in an OOM error.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Resource exhaustion [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenial-of-service[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m via uncontrolled memory allocation in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfont parsing.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations and Findings  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The exception originates in `org.apache.fontbox.pfb.PfbParser.parsePfb`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating that the PFB parsing logic attempts to load or buffer too much data.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The stack trace flows through `Type1Font.createWithPFB` and into PDFBox [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfont-related classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDType1Font`, `PDFontFactory`, `PDResources`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The PDF content stream operator `SetFontAndSize` triggers font loading, which [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis ultimately responsible for invoking the PFB parser.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The crash is reproducible with a specified heap size [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-Xmx1710m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, suggesting[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe input exercises extreme memory usage rather than a trivial leak.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness itself [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m merely [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39morchestrates PDF loading and text stripping; it is not the root cause but the entry[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoint.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To gain a holistic understanding of this issue, focus on:  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `org.apache.fontbox.pfb.PfbParser`: parsing logic and buffering strategy for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPFB segments  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `org.apache.fontbox.type1.Type1Font.createWithPFB`: how PFB data is handed off [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto the font representation  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.font.PDType1Font` and `PDFontFactory`: integration [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m fonts into the PDF model  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `PDResources.getFont` and the `SetFontAndSize` operator in `PDFStreamEngine`: [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhow fonts are requested and instantiated during page processing  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Overall memory usage patterns when loading large or malformed font streams  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInvestigating these areas will clarify how PFB data is consumed and why it can lead[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto unbounded memory allocation.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m213[0m[39m:                    int length2 = [0m[1;35mstream.getInt[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSName.LENGTH2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m214[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m215[0m[39m:                    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m repair Length1 and Length2 if necessary[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m216[0m[39m:                    byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m bytes = [0m[1;35mfontFile.toByteArray[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m217[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes.length == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m218[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m219[0m[39m:                        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Font data unavailable"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m220[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m221[0m[39m:                    length1 = [0m[1;35mrepairLength1[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes, length1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m222[0m[39m:                    length2 = [0m[1;35mrepairLength2[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes, length1, length2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m223[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m224[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m & [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == PFB_START_MARKER[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m225[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m226[0m[39m:                        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m some bad files embed the entire PFB, see PDFBOX-[0m[1;36m2607[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m227[0m[39m:                        t1 = [0m[1;35mType1Font.createWithPFB[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m228[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m229[0m[39m:                    else[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m230[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m231[0m[39m:                        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m the PFB embedded as two segments back-to-back[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m232[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength1 < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || length1 > length1 + length2[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m233[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m234[0m[39m:                            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid length data, actual [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mlength: "[0m[39m +[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m235[0m[39m:                                    bytes.length + [0m[32m", /Length1: "[0m[39m + length1 + [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m", /Length2: "[0m[39m + length2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m236[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m237[0m[39m:                        byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m segment1 = [0m[1;35mArrays.copyOfRange[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m238[0m[39m:                        byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m segment2 = [0m[1;35mArrays.copyOfRange[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes, length1, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength1 + length2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m239[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m240[0m[39m:                        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m empty streams are simply ignored[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m241[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength1 > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && length2 > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m242[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m243[0m[39m:                            t1 = [0m[1;35mType1Font.createWithSegments[0m[1;39m([0m[39msegment1, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegment2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m244[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m245[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m246[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m247[0m[39m:                catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDamagedFontException e[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m248[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m249[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mLOG.warn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> [0m[32m"Can't read damaged embedded Type1 font "[0m[39m + [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mfd.getFontName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m250[0m[39m:                    fontIsDamaged = true;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/pfb/PfbParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:68[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m75[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:     * Heuristically chosen max length to buffer a Type1 font[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:    private static final long MAX_LENGTH = 100_000_000;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:     * the parsed pfb-data.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The root cause is that PfbParser’s `InputStream` and `String` constructors call [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mreadAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor `Files.readAllBytes`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, loading the entire PFB data into memory[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore any size checks, causing OOM on large/malformed inputs. Although `parsePfb` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menforces `MAX_LENGTH`, it only applies after buffering everything. We will enforce [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same `MAX_LENGTH` limit at the point of initial data ingestion.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Points  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m103[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m107[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString filename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m93[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m96[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` constructor – add a pre-check to catch oversized [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte arrays immediately.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Introduce a bounded-read helper that enforces the existing `MAX_LENGTH` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstant before buffering:  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In `PfbParser.java`, add a private static method [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mreadAllBytesWithLimit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream in, long max[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` that reads the stream in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfixed-size chunks [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m KB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, tracks the cumulative byte count, and throws an [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` if the count exceeds `max`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Modify the constructors to use this helper:  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In `public [0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Replace `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m pfb = [0m[1;35min.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpfb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • With `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m pfb = [0m[1;35mreadAllBytesWithLimit[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, MAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpfb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In `public [0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString filename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Open the file via `[0m[1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtry-with-resources block.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Delegate to the `InputStream` constructor, so it benefits from the same [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlimit. Remove `Files.readAllBytes`.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In `public [0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • At the top, insert:  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes.length > MAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"PFB data too large: "[0m[39m + bytes.length [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                    + [0m[32m" bytes, exceeds max "[0m[39m + MAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          This prevents unbounded memory use if callers supply a huge byte array.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserving Critical Logic  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remains unchanged, retaining the per‐segment `MAX_LENGTH` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menforcement already implemented.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The new helper enforces the same `MAX_LENGTH` value to ensure consistency.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to the harness, PDFStreamEngine, Type1Font parsing logic, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor downstream APIs, so existing functionality and tests remain intact.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Error Handling & Fuzzer Behavior  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Oversized or malicious PFB inputs now trigger an `IOException: PFB data too [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlarge`, which is caught in `PDType1Font`’s font‐loading logic and logged as a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdamaged font.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer will see a benign exception rather than an OOM, avoiding heap [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustion while preserving the execution path.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Legitimate fonts slightly over [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m MB in PFB format will be rejected. To [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madjust, increase `MAX_LENGTH` accordingly, but keep it bounded to prevent DoS.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The helper uses chunked reads; performance impact is minimal since PFB files [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare normally <<[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m MB.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References in Codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing `MAX_LENGTH` constant [0m[1;39m([0m[39m100_000_000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is already tuned as the upper[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbound in `parsePfb`.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar bounded‐read patterns are used elsewhere in PDFBox [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., CFF/CID [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstream readers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to prevent unbounded memory growth.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. Summary of Changes  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add `readAllBytesWithLimit` helper [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPfbParser.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Refactor constructors in PfbParser to use this helper or pre‐check `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications to external libraries, harness code, or test code.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing tests should pass, and the fuzzer will no longer trigger an OOM [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon malicious PFB inputs.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Introduced `private static byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m [0m[1;35mreadAllBytesWithLimit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream in, long [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Reads in [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m KB chunks into a `ByteArrayOutputStream`.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Tracks cumulative bytes read; throws `IOException` if `totalRead > max`.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Updated two constructors of `PfbParser`:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString filename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`: replaced `[0m[1;35mFiles.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstreaming via `readAllBytesWithLimit`.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`: replaced `[0m[1;35min.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`readAllBytesWithLimit`.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In the `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` constructor, added a check to throw [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` if `bytes.length > MAX_LENGTH`.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mResult After Patch  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Running the same fuzzer input still produces:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The crash now occurs at `[0m[1;35mPfbParser.parsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPfbParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:198[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`—inside the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing logic, not during the raw data read.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The patch successfully caps raw input size but does not prevent large internal [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocations during parsing.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **parsePfb Method**  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How section lengths are interpreted and used to allocate arrays.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are any unbounded loops or array-copy operations that multiply [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory usage.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Internal buffers or data structures that expand based on header-declared [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msizes.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **PFB Segment Handling**  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Validation of segment headers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., ASCII vs. binary sections[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before memory [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Possible discrepancies between declared lengths and actual data.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Integration with Type1Font.createWithPFB**  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any additional conversions or buffering performed after parsing that could [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexacerbate memory usage.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Overall Memory Lifecycle**  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Points at which parsed data is retained in memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `pfbdata` field[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Opportunities to stream or lazily process segments rather than loading all at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monce.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis evaluation shows that while input-size limiting is necessary, the core parser [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic in `[0m[1;35mPfbParser.parsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` must also be reviewed for unbounded allocations [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand defensive validation of PFB data.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m95[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcorrupt?[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m synthetic font[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m96[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"FontDirectory"[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m108[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m font dict[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m109[0m[39m:        int length = [0m[1;35mread[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.INTEGER[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.intValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m110[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mread[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME, [0m[32m"dict"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m111[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m found in some TeX fonts[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m112[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mreadMaybe[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME, [0m[32m"dup"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m113[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m if present, the [0m[32m"currentdict"[0m[39m is not required[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m114[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mread[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME, [0m[32m"begin"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m115[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m116[0m[39m:        for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < length; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m117[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m118[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m premature end[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m119[0m[39m:            Token token = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m120[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtoken == null[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/pfb/PfbParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:155[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m165[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m155[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m156[0m[39m:            int size = [0m[1;35min.read[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m157[0m[39m:            size += [0m[1;35min.read[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m << [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m158[0m[39m:            size += [0m[1;35min.read[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m << [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m159[0m[39m:            size += [0m[1;35min.read[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m << [0m[1;36m24[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m160[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mLOG.debug[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"record type: [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m, segment size: [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m, recordType, size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m161[0m[39m:            long newTotal = total + size;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m162[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnewTotal > MAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:                throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"record size would be too large: "[0m[39m + [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnewTotal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m164[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m165[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/pfb/PfbParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:103[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m107[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m103[0m[39m:    public [0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal InputStream in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m104[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m:        byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m pfb = [0m[1;35min.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m106[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpfb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m107[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Analyze & Identify Root Causes[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing patch caps only the *total* PFB input length, but **does not** [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent the parser from allocating very large byte‐arrays per PFB segment or [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmerging all segments into one large array [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`pfbdata`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, causing an OOM during [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - PFB files are expected to contain exactly three segments [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASCII header, binary[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata, ASCII trailer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  The parser currently treats *any* number of segments until [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEOF, so a malformed input could trigger dozens of segments, each with a nonzero [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength, multiplying peak memory usage.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no per‐segment size bound: a single segment size [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom the [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m‐byte [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m could be near `MAX_LENGTH` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m100[0m[39m MB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, leading to middle‐loop allocation of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and finally `new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtotal[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, pushing peak heap usage above safe [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlimits.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The raw‐read constructors [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mPfbParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill read the whole input into a byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m first; combined with segment buffers and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe merged array, this triples memory usage.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Critical Logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue reading all three PFB segments, reorder ASCII/binary/ASCII [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegments, and build `pfbdata` for use by downstream `Type1Parser`.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter public APIs or test harnesses.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We keep the existing `MAX_LENGTH` constant and streaming‐read helpers; we [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimply tighten validation inside `parsePfb`.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Concrete Patch Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Introduce a **per‐segment length check** immediately after decoding the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m-byte `size` field:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m after computing [0m[32m'size'[0m[39m:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || size > MAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"PFB segment size invalid or too large: "[0m[39m + size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Enforce the **spec-mandated segment count** of at most three segments:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int segmentCount = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      do [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          segmentCount++;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39msegmentCount > [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Too many PFB segments: "[0m[39m + segmentCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m existing EOF/marker checks[0m[33m...[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Keep the existing **cumulative total** check [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`newTotal > MAX_LENGTH`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbound the sum of all segments.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Optionally, to reduce peak memory, **release intermediate buffers** right [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter merging:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m after pfbdata = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtotal[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39mcopy segments[0m[33m...[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mbarrList.clear[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m allow prior segment arrays to be GC'ed[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. No changes to harness or external tests; constructors and downstream logic [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain identical.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Why This Fix Works[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Per-segment cap** prevents the worst cases where a single segment header [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemands a huge allocation under the total limit.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Segment-count limit** guards against cleverly malformed inputs that pack [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmany small segments [0m[1;39m([0m[39m→ many buffers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m even if their total is within MAX_LENGTH.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Combined with the existing total‐length guard, this makes it impossible for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to allocate any arrays [0m[1;39m([0m[39mraw input + segment buffers + merged [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`pfbdata`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m whose sum exceeds roughly `[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m × MAX_LENGTH`, which on a modern JVM with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgigabytes of heap will avoid OOM on fuzzing inputs up to [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m MB.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Throwing an `IOException` on any size violation replaces the unchecked OOM [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith a controlled failure path, which fuzzers and production code can handle [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgracefully.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid PFB files with more than three pseudo-segments [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrare[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now be [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrejected; this is conformant to the PFB spec.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Very large but legitimate single segments [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m MB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are still refused; if [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musers need larger PFBs, `MAX_LENGTH` can be tuned in a minor release, but defaults [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould prioritize safety.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests expecting arbitrary PFB sizes beyond the cap will need updates; however,[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in Codebase[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
